// Calculates a heuristic frequency for words not in the list
function estimatedFreq(word) {
	// Words of rating 10 have an average length of 8.21 characters
	var estimate = 10 / (Math.abs(word.length-8.21) + 1);
	return estimate;
}

// Function to extract a list of words from a string
function getWords(string) {
	words = string.split(/[^\w'\-]+/);
	if (words[0] == '') words.shift();
	if (words[words.length-1] == '') words.pop();
	return words;
}

var tag_ratings = new Object();
// Function to sort words by their ratings
function rateSort(a, b) {
	return tag_ratings[b] - tag_ratings[a];
}

// Function to generate the tags (must be done after the post has been written)
function generateTags() {
	// Get text of current post and strip HTML, links and [quote] bbCode
	var text = document.getElementById(editorId).value;
	text = text.replace(/<[^>]+>/g, ' ').replace(/[a-z]+:\/\/[^ ]*/g, '');
	var temp = document.createElement('div');
	temp.innerHTML = text;
	text = temp.textContent.replace(/\[quote(\s+user="[^"]*")?\]|\[\/quote\]/g, '');
	// Make a list of words, delete empty words at beginning or end
	var words = getWords(text);
	// Count and rate frequency of words
	var word_ratings = new Object();
	i = 0;
	while (i < words.length) {
		word = words[i].toLowerCase();
		if (word in word_ratings) {
			words.splice(i, 1);
			word_ratings[word] += 1;
		} else {
			words[i] = word;
			word_ratings[word] = 1;
			i++;
		}
	}
	for (var word in word_ratings) {
		if (freq[word]) word_ratings[word] /= freq[word]
		// Use a heuristic for words not in the list
		else word_ratings[word] /= estimatedFreq(word);
	}
	// Get array of all the tags, and rate them
	var tags = document.getElementById(allTagsId).value.split('&');
	for (var i = 0; i < tags.length; i++) {
		tags[i] = decodeURIComponent(tags[i].replace(/\+/g, ' '));

		tag_words = getWords(tags[i]);
		tag_rating = 0;
		for (j = 0; j < tag_words.length; j++) {
			word = tag_words[j].toLowerCase();
			if (word in word_ratings) tag_rating += word_ratings[word]
			else if (word in freq) tag_rating -= 1/freq[word]
			else tag_rating -= 1/estimatedFreq(word)
		}
		if (tag_rating > 0) tag_rating /= tag_words.length;
		tag_ratings[tags[i]] = tag_rating;

		tags.splice(i+1, 1);
	}
	tags.sort(rateSort);
	// A cutoff event horizon I pulled out of my arse
	var horizon = 0.00002;
	if (tag_ratings[tags[0]] < horizon)
		alert('No relevant tags found.');
	else {
		// Choose tag_count or less most relevant tags
		var tag_string = tags[0];
		for (i = 1; i < tag_count; i++) {
			if (tag_ratings[tags[i]] < horizon) break;
			tag_string += ', ' + tags[i];
		}
		tagInput.value = tag_string;
	}
}

// Add a button for the tag generator
var tagInput = document.getElementById(tagInputId);
button = document.createElement('button');
button.textContent = 'Automatically find relevant tags';
button.type = 'button';
button.addEventListener('click', generateTags, false);
tagInput.parentNode.appendChild(button);
